# LKM Info

A simple tool for parsing linux kernel and loadable kernel module binary files.

## Build

```
$ python3 -m venv .env
$ source .env/bin/activate
$ (.env) pip install -r requirements.txt
```

## Run

```
$ (.env) python -m lvminfo verify -k <kernel> -s <kallsyms> -m <ko>
```
